<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожалеть.html>сожале́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sožalétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожаление.html>сожале́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sožalénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожаление.html>сожале́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожаление.html>сожале́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожаление.html>сожале́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>regret
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сожаление.html>сожале́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k sožaléniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">regretfully, regrettably</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>pity</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сожалеть.html>сожале́ть</a> (8828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожалеть.html>сожале́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sožalétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pity, to be sorry <i>(for smb.)</i></li>
<li>to regret, to deplore, to be sorry <i>(that)</i></li></ol>

***сожжение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сожжение.html>сожже́ние</a> (27376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сожг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sožg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожжение.html>сожже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sožžénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожжение.html>сожже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожжение.html>сожже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожжение.html>сожже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>burning, burning up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сожительство.html>сожи́тельство</a> (28845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожительство.html>сожи́тельство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sožítelʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожительство.html>сожи́тельства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожительство.html>сожи́тельства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожительство.html>сожи́тельств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cohabitation <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of two lovers</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; common-law marriage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> living under one roof; living together as roommates</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coexistence as neighbors
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:братский.html>бра́тское</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сожительство.html>сожи́тельство</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">brátskoje <b>sožítelʹstvo</b> nášix naródov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the brotherly <b>coexistence</b> of our peoples</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cohabitation <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of a president and a prime minister from different parties</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***сожрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сожрать.html>сожра́ть</a> (7761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жрать.html>жрать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожрать.html>сожра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sožrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жрать.html>жрать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сожрать.html>сожра́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:торт.html>торт</a>?!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty <b>sožrál</b> vesʹ tort?!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Have you eaten all the cake?!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gorge, to scarf down <i>(overeat or eat greedily, immodestly)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:съесть.html>съе́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сожрать.html>сожра́л</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ne sʺjel, a <b>sožrál</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He didn't eat—he made a pig of himself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of an insect</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sting, to bite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>комары́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сожрать.html>сожра́ли</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Komarý <b>sožráli</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Mosquitos have stung me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:созвать.html>созва́ть</a> (14060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созвать.html>созва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sozvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созывать.html>созыва́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сзыва́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to call <i>(together)</i>, to summon, to invite</li>
<li>to call, to convene, to convoke

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здие</a> (10421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvezdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">constellātiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sozvézdije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>constellation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здия</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:современный.html>совреме́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:астрономия.html>астроно́мии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:участок.html>уча́стки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разделённый.html>разделена́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небесный.html>небе́сная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сфера.html>сфе́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удобство.html>удо́бства</a> ориентирования <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звездный.html>звёздном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бе</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древность.html>дре́вности</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:созвездие.html>созве́здиями</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:называться.html>называ́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>характерные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ры</a>, образуемые <a href = vnd.unilang:яркий.html>я́ркими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёздами</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Sozvézdija</b> — v sovreménnoj astronómii učástki, na kotóryje razdelená nebésnaja sféra dlja udóbstva orijentirovanija na zvjózdnom nébe. V drévnosti <b>sozvézdijami</b> nazyválisʹ xarakternyje figúry, obrazujemyje járkimi zvjózdami.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Constellations in the modern astronomy are areas dividing the celestial sphere for convenient orientation in the stellar sky. In the ancient times the distinctive shapes formed by bright stars were called constellations</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***создававший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:создавать.html>создава́вший</a> (1857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***создавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:создавать.html>создава́ть</a> (1857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создать.html>созда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sozdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создавать.html>создава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sozdavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создать.html>созда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to create</li>
<li>to found, to originate</li>
<li>to set up, to establish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:создатель.html>созда́тель</a> (6733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создать.html>созда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sozdátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to create</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создатель.html>созда́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sozdátelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создатель.html>созда́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создатель.html>созда́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создатель.html>созда́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">созда́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>creator (one who creates)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***создать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:создать.html>созда́ть</a> (733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">съзьдати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭzĭdati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to build, to erect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъzьdati</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zьdati</i>. The modern conjugation is analogical after <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, replacing the old present stem <i>созижд</i>-.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создать.html>созда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sozdátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создавать.html>создава́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созидать.html>созида́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to create</li>
<li>to found, to originate</li>
<li>to set up, to establish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to build, to erect</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The imperfectives <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создавать.html>создава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sozdavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созидать.html>созида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sozidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> have the same meaning, but the latter is literary or dated.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создаваться.html>создава́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sozdavátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создаться.html>созда́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sozdátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воссоздать.html>воссозда́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vossozdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:созерцать.html>созерца́емый</a> (18119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ние</a> (15439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созерцать.html>созерца́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sozercátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sozercánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contemplation
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1866</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fydor_Dostoyevsky" class="extiw" title="w:Fydor Dostoyevsky">Fydor Dostoyevsky</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crime_and_Punishment" class="extiw" title="w:Crime and Punishment">Crime and Punishment</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскольник.html>раско́льников</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неподвижный.html>неподви́жно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрываться.html>отрыва́ясь</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переходить.html>переходи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёзы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ние</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мал</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> кака́я-то <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чила</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Raskólʹnikov sidél, smotrél nepodvížno, ne otryvájasʹ; myslʹ jevó perexodíla v grjózy, v <b>sozercánije</b>; on ni o čóm ne dúmal, no kakája-to toská volnovála jevó i múčila.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Raskolnikov sat there, unmoving, staring fixedly. His thought passed into dreams, into <b>contemplation</b>; he did not think about anything, but some melancholy worried and tormented him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***созидать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:созидать.html>созида́ть</a> (23247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зида́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создать.html>созда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sozdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сознать.html>созна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
